<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">BENEFICIAL BANCORP,&nbsp;INC. ANNOUNCES SECOND QUARTER RESULTS</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">PHILADELPHIA, PENNSYLVANIA, July&nbsp;23, 2015 &#151; Beneficial Bancorp,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Beneficial&#148;) (NASDAQ GS: BNCL), the parent company of Beneficial Bank (the &#147;Bank&#148;), today announced its financial results for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; Beneficial recorded net income of $7.1 million and $12.3 million, or $0.09 and $0.16 per diluted share, for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, respectively, compared to net income of $4.6 million and $7.0 million, or $0.06 and $0.09 per diluted share, for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Highlights for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 are as follows:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Net income increased 54.2% and 74.6% for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to the same periods in 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Our net interest margin improved to 2.83% for the second quarter of 2015 compared to 2.75% for the first quarter of 2015 and 2.81% for the second quarter of 2014.&#160; Loan growth, increases in non-interest bearing deposits, and reductions in higher-cost time deposits and borrowings are the primary drivers of the improvement in our net interest margin.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Continued asset quality improvement and net loan recoveries resulted in a $1.6 million negative provision for loan losses during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; Our allowance for loan losses totaled $47.8 million, or 1.76% of total loans and 124.87% of non-performing loans at June&nbsp;30, 2015, compared to $49.1 million, or 1.84% of total loans and 128.70% of non-performing loans, at March&nbsp;31, 2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On a linked quarter basis, our loan portfolio grew $42.5 million (6.4% annualized growth) as a result of increases in commercial real estate and commercial business loans as well as a $14.4 million purchase of residential mortgage loans.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, our loan portfolio increased $286.8 million, or 11.8%, primarily due to purchases of multi-family and residential loans, as well as organic growth primarily in our commercial loan portfolio.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Core deposits remained stable at $2.7 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 and December&nbsp;31, 2014, excluding the second-step proceeds, despite $70.8 million in planned decreases in higher-cost, non-relationship-based municipal accounts during the period.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Following the second-step conversion that was completed on January&nbsp;12, 2015, our capital levels increased and remained strong with tangible capital to tangible assets totaling 21.14% at June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to 20.83% at March&nbsp;31, 2015 and 10.44% at December&nbsp;31, 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tangible book value per share totaled $11.77 at June&nbsp;30, 2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">1<a name="PB_1_211552_3873"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\108736\15-16075-1\task7499879\16075-1-mm-01.htm',USER='108736',CD='Jul 22 23:49 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are pleased with the progress our team made against a number of goals during the second quarter&#148; said Gerard Cuddy, Beneficial&#146;s President and CEO.&nbsp; &#147;Improvement in our balance sheet mix, loan growth, net interest income, and net interest margin all contributed to our success. Our focus remains on employee engagement, a superior customer experience, prudent capital management and organic growth to continue to improve the financial performance of our organization.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Balance Sheet</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total assets decreased $15.0 million, or 0.3%, to $4.74 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to $4.75 billion at December&nbsp;31, 2014. &#160;Cash and cash equivalents decreased $247.7 million to $286.3 million at June&nbsp;30, 2015 from $534.0 million at December&nbsp;31, 2014.&#160; The decrease in cash and cash equivalents was primarily driven by the deployment of a portion of the second-step conversion offering proceeds through the participation in a portfolio of multi-family loans during the first quarter and the purchase of residential real estate loans during the year as well as organic loan growth.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments decreased $50.1 million, or 3.4%, to $1.44 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to $1.49 billion at December&nbsp;31, 2014.&#160; We continue to focus on maintaining a high quality investment portfolio that provides a steady stream of cash flows both in the current and in rising interest rate environments. We are also focused on improving our balance sheet mix by reducing the percentage of our assets in cash and investments and growing our loan portfolio.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Loans increased $286.8 million, or 11.8%, to $2.71 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 from $2.42 billion at December&nbsp;31, 2014.&#160; The increase was primarily due to a $200.1 million participation in a portfolio of multi-family loans and the purchase of $35.4 million of residential real estate loans. The remaining increase was due to growth in our commercial real estate and commercial business loans, which include shared national credits.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deposits decreased $504.6 million, or 13.0%, to $3.38 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 from $3.88 billion at December&nbsp;31, 2014.&#160; Deposits at December&nbsp;31, 2014 included $482.1 million of subscription funds held in deposit accounts in connection with the second-step conversion offering that were reclassified into stockholders&#146; equity in the first quarter of 2015. Excluding the $482.1 million of subscription funds, deposits decreased $22.5 million during the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015. The $22.5 million decrease in deposits during the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 was primarily due to a $70.8 million decrease in municipal deposits and a $28.6 million decrease in time deposits, which resulted from our planned run-off of higher-cost, non-relationship-based accounts.&#160; The decrease in deposits was partially offset by increases in savings deposits, as well as interest and non-interest bearing checking deposits.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Stockholders&#146; equity increased $490.9 million, or 80.4%, to $1.10 billion at June&nbsp;30, 2015 from $610.9 million at December&nbsp;31, 2014.&#160; The increase in stockholders&#146; equity was primarily due to net proceeds received in connection with the second-step conversion that was completed during the first quarter of 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net Interest Income</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, net interest income was $31.2 million, an increase of $2.0 million, or 6.9%, from the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. The increase in net interest income was primarily due to higher interest earning assets as a result of the second-step conversion proceeds. During 2015, these proceeds were partially utilized to increase the loan portfolio, which resulted in an increase in the average balance of loans. Net interest income was also positively impacted by a reduction in the average cost of liabilities primarily due to reductions in higher-cost time deposits and borrowings, which offset the decline in yields on loans and investments. The net interest margin totaled 2.83% for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 as compared to 2.81% for the same period in 2014. We expect that the continued low interest rate environment will put pressure on the net interest margin in future periods but we are focused on growing our loan portfolio and improving our balance sheet mix to help stabilize our net interest margin.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Beneficial reported net interest income of $61.4 million, an increase of $2.6 million, or 4.4%, from the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. The increase in net interest income was primarily due to higher interest earning assets as a result of the second-step conversion proceeds. During 2015, these proceeds</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">2<a name="PB_2_211624_5335"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\108736\15-16075-1\task7499879\16075-1-mm-01.htm',USER='108736',CD='Jul 22 23:49 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">were utilized to increase the loan portfolio, which resulted in an increase in the average balance of loans. Net interest income was also positively impacted by a reduction in the average cost of liabilities and a $169.8 million decrease in the average balance of municipal deposits, partially offset by a decline in yields on loans and investments.&#160; Our net interest margin decreased to 2.79% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 from 2.81% for the same period in 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Non-interest Income</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, non-interest income totaled $7.2 million, an increase of $853 thousand, or 13.5%, from the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. Service charges and other income increased $922 thousand during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to the same period a year ago primarily due to increases of $754 thousand in limited partnership income and $223 thousand in foreign ATM fees.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, non-interest income totaled $12.8 million, an increase of $857 thousand, or 7.2%, from the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. Service charges and other income increased $1.2 million during the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to the same period a year ago as a result of increases of $958 thousand in limited partnership income and $448 thousand in foreign ATM fees. These increases were partially offset by a $306 thousand decrease in the net gain on the sale of investment securities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Non-interest Expense</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, non-interest expense totaled $30.0 million, an increase of $785 thousand, or 2.7% from the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; The increase in non-interest expense was primarily driven by a $1.1 million increase in salaries and employee benefits due to merit increases and other retirement benefits, a $412 thousand increase in marketing expenses due to current year initiatives to continue rebranding and drive future growth and a $263 thousand increase in professional fees.&#160; These increases were partially offset by a $225 thousand decrease in occupancy expense, a $293 thousand decrease in Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (&#147;FDIC&#148;) insurance expense due to lower assessments, and a $420 thousand decrease in debit card rewards expense due to changes in the program parameters.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, non-interest expense remained relatively consistent at $60.5 million, an increase of $41 thousand, or 0.1%, from the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. The slight increase in non-interest expense was primarily driven by a $1.5 million increase in salaries and employee benefits due to merit increases and other retirement benefits, an $843 thousand increase in marketing expenses due to current year initiatives to continue rebranding and drive future growth and a $463 thousand increase in professional fees.&#160; These increases were partially offset by a $1.3 million decrease in operating expenses related to the headquarters move in the first quarter of 2014, a $528 thousand decrease in FDIC insurance expense due to lower assessments, and a $642 thousand decrease in debit card rewards expense due to changes in the program parameters.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Income Taxes</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, we recorded a provision for income taxes of $2.9 million, reflecting an effective tax rate of 29.5% compared to a provision for income taxes of $1.5 million, reflecting an effective tax benefit of 24.7% for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, we recorded a provision for income taxes of $5.0 million, reflecting an effective tax rate of 28.7%, compared to a provision for income taxes of $1.4 million, reflecting an effective tax rate of 16.9% for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. The increase in income tax expense and the effective tax rate during these periods is due to higher profitability levels and ratio of taxable income compared to tax exempt income for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 as compared to the same periods in 2014.&#160; The effective tax rates differ from the statutory rate of 35% principally because of tax-exempt investments, non-taxable income related to bank-owned life insurance and tax credits received on affordable housing partnerships. These tax credits relate to investments maintained by the Bank as a limited partner in partnerships that sponsor affordable housing projects utilizing low-income housing credits pursuant to Section&nbsp;42 of the Internal Revenue Code.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">3<a name="PB_3_211649_5796"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Asset Quality</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Asset quality metrics continued to improve as non-performing loans, excluding government guaranteed student loans, decreased to $12.8 million at June&nbsp;30, 2015, compared to $14.6 million at December&nbsp;31, 2014, and $27.8 million at June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; The $15.0 million, or 54.0%, decrease from June&nbsp;30, 2014 in non-performing loans, was the result of our continued work out of non-performing assets as well as $12.3 million of non-performing commercial loan sales during the third and fourth quarter of 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a result of the improvement in our asset quality metrics and net recoveries received during the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, we recorded a $1.6 million negative provision for loan losses for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to recording a $250 thousand provision for loan losses for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; Net recoveries totaled $248 thousand during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 compared to net charge-offs of $1.7 million during the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Bank&#146;s allowance for loan losses totaled $47.8 million, or 1.76% of total loans, compared to $50.7 million, or 2.09% of total loans, at December&nbsp;31, 2014, and $52.6 million, or 2.22% of total loans at June&nbsp;30, 2014.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Capital</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Bank&#146;s capital position remains strong relative to current regulatory requirements. The Bank continues to have substantial liquidity that has been retained in cash or invested in high quality government-backed securities.&#160; In addition, at June&nbsp;30, 2015, we had the ability to borrow up to $1.4 billion combined from the Federal Home Loan Bank of Pittsburgh and the Federal Reserve Bank of Philadelphia. Our capital ratios are considered to be well capitalized and are as follows:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Maintaining strong capital levels remains one of our top priorities.&#160; Our capital levels are in excess of well capitalized levels under Basel III regulatory requirements.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">About Beneficial Bancorp,&nbsp;Inc.</font></u></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Beneficial is a community-based, diversified financial services company providing consumer and commercial banking services. Its principal subsidiary, Beneficial Bank, has served individuals and businesses in the Delaware Valley area since 1853. The Bank is the oldest and largest bank headquartered in Philadelphia, Pennsylvania, with 56 offices in the greater Philadelphia and South New Jersey regions. Insurance services are offered through the Beneficial Insurance Services, LLC and wealth management services are offered through the Beneficial Advisors, LLC, both wholly owned subsidiaries of the Bank. For more information about the Bank and Beneficial, please visit www.thebeneficial.com.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">BENEFICIAL BANCORP,&nbsp;INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(Dollars in thousands, except per share amounts)</font></b></p>
